<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фига.html>фи́га</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fíga</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fig</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фиговый.html>фи́говый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fígovyj</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фигура.html>фигу́ра</a> (1135)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фигура.html>фигу́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">figúra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фигура.html>фигу́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фигура.html>фигу́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фигура.html>фигу́р</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>figure
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фигура.html>фигу́ра</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:высший.html>вы́сшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пилотаж.html>пилота́жа</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>figúra</b> výsševo pilotáža</i> ― <span class="e-translation">aerobatic stunt</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видный.html>ви́дная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:фигура.html>фигу́ра</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vídnaja <b>figúra</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">prominent <b>figure</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ключевой.html>ключева́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:фигура.html>фигу́ра</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ključevája <b>figúra</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">key <b>figure</b> (as in an important person)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chess</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> piece</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> face card</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фигурировать.html>фигури́ровать</a> (12257)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">figurieren</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фигура.html>фигу́ра</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">figúra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***физиология.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:физиология.html>физиоло́гия</a> (13954)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:физиология.html>физиоло́гия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fiziológija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:физиология.html>физиоло́гии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:физиология.html>физиоло́гии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:физиология.html>физиоло́гий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>physiology</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">физио́лог</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">fiziólog</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:физиологический.html>физиологи́ческий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">fiziologíčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:физиономия.html>физионо́мия</a> (3360)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:физиономия.html>физионо́мия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fizionómija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:физиономия.html>физионо́мии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:физиономия.html>физионо́мии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:физиономия.html>физионо́мий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>grimace, facial expression, mien</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> face, phis</li></ol>

***физкультура.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:физкультура.html>физкульту́ра</a> (9281)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A clipping of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">физ(ическая)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fiz(ičeskaja)</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">physical</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:культура.html>культу́ра</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kulʹtúra</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">culture</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:физкультура.html>физкульту́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fizkulʹtúra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:физкультура.html>физкульту́ры</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>physical education</li></ol>

***фиксировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фиксировать.html>фикси́ровать</a> (10134)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фиксировать.html>фикси́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fiksírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:фиксировать.html>фикси́ровать</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зафиксировать.html>зафикси́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fix, to set, to settle, to state</li>
<li>to record</li>
<li>to fix <i>(a photograph)</i></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фиксировать.html>фикси́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fiksírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фиксироваться.html>фикси́роваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fiksírovatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:фиксироваться.html>фикси́роваться</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зафикси́роваться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to register
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́мя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b>зафикси́ровалось</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:память.html>па́мяти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jejó ímja ne <b>zafiksírovalosʹ</b> u menjá v pámjati</i> ― <span class="e-translation">her name didn't register on me</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">psychology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fixate <i>(on)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фиксировать.html>фикси́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fiksírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:филиал.html>филиа́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">filiál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:филиал.html>филиа́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:филиал.html>филиа́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:филиал.html>филиа́лов</a></b>)
